SELECT [s].[MSSV], [s].[HoTen], [s].[NgaySinh], [s].[GioiTinh], [d].[Name] AS [Department], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolYear], [s1].[Name] AS [StudyProgram], [a].[HouseNumber] AS [AddressNhanThu_HouseNumber], [a].[StreetName] AS [AddressNhanThu_StreetName], [a].[Ward] AS [AddressNhanThu_Ward], [a].[District] AS [AddressNhanThu_District], [a].[Country] AS [AddressNhanThu_Country], [a0].[HouseNumber] AS [AddressThuongTru_HouseNumber], [a0].[StreetName] AS [AddressThuongTru_StreetName], [a0].[Ward] AS [AddressThuongTru_Ward], [a0].[District] AS [AddressThuongTru_District], [a0].[Country] AS [AddressThuongTru_Country], [a1].[HouseNumber] AS [AddressTamTru_HouseNumber], [a1].[StreetName] AS [AddressTamTru_StreetName], [a1].[Ward] AS [AddressTamTru_Ward], [a1].[District] AS [AddressTamTru_District], [a1].[Country] AS [AddressTamTru_Country], [s].[Email], [s].[SoDienThoai], [s].[QuocTich], [i].[IdentificationType] AS [Identification_Type], [i].[Number] AS [Identification_Number], [i].[IssueDate] AS [Identification_IssueDate], [i].[ExpiryDate] AS [Identification_ExpiryDate], [i].[IssuedBy] AS [Identification_IssuedBy], [i].[IssuingCountry] AS [Identification_IssuingCountry], [i].[Notes] AS [Identification_Notes], [s2].[Name] AS [Status]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [Departments] AS [d] ON [s].[DepartmentId] = [d].[Id]
INNER JOIN [SchoolYears] AS [s0] ON [s].[SchoolYearId] = [s0].[Id]
INNER JOIN [StudyPrograms] AS [s1] ON [s].[StudyProgramId] = [s1].[Id]
